class="FeatureContent_body__NTf8M"><p class="ArticleBodyText_articleBodyContent__17wqE typography_articleBody__3UcBa" data-component="paragraph">Donald Trump<!-- --> feels threatened, all the time. “I think everything’s a threat,” he <a class="media-ui-Link_link-tVkXhPLPofs-" data-component="link" href="https://rollcall.com/factbase/trump/transcript/donald-trump-interview-john-micklethwait-bloomberg-detroit-economic-club-october-15-2024/" rel="noopener" target="_blank" title="Interview: John Micklethwait of Bloomberg Interviews Donald Trump in Chicago - October 15, 2024">said</a> at the Economic Club of Chicago recently. “There’s nothing that’s not a threat.”<br/><br/>He’s threatened by “woke” businesses.<br/><br/>He’s threatened by global trade and diplomacy.</p><p class="ArticleBodyText_articleBodyContent__17wqE typography_articleBody__3UcBa" data-component="paragraph">He’s threatened by an independent Federal Reserve.<br/><br/>He’s threatened by China (but not Russia).<br/><br/>He’s threatened by voting and voters.<br/><br/>He’s threatened by immigrants, undocumented workers and people of color.<br/><br/>He’s threatened by women, reproductive rights and <!-- -->Kamala Harris<!-- -->.<br/><br/>He’s threatened by law enforcement, schools, the media, the government, big cities, big tech, facts, civility, germs, the weather, sharks and windmills.<br/><br/>Unlike the rest of us, Trump has myriad tools at his disposal to help conquer his fears — particularly if he revisits the Oval Office.</p><div class="media-ui-Placeholder_placeholderParagraphWrapper-yqk1PvmrNoc-"><div class="media-ui-Placeholder_shimmeringParagraph-CAmHW46Yvo4-"
